***buster.html

***buzzard.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buzzard.html>buzzard</a> (94768)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">buisart</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">buison</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">buson</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">buse</i>), <a href = vnd.unilang:possibly.html>possibly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">buteō</i>.
</p>

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">kaleidoscope</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">καλός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kalós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beautiful.html>beautiful</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εἶδος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eîdos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:shape.html>shape</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-oid</i>)  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-scope</i>. <p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> Calicut, <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:india.html>India</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:where.html>where</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cloth.html>cloth</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:originally.html>originally</a> exported, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malayalam" class="extiw" title="w:Malayalam">Malayalam</a></span> <i class="Mlym mention" lang="ml">കോഴിക്കോട്</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ml-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kōḻikkōṭŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Kozhikode</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Mlym mention" lang="ml">കോഴി</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ml-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kōḻi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:palace.html>palace</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Mlym mention" lang="ml">ക്കോട്</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ml-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kkōṭŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fortified <a href = vnd.unilang:palace.html>palace</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:y.html>y</a>’ replaced <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> interchangeable ‘zh’.
